 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>NEWS RELEASE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTHUR J. GALLAGHER&nbsp;&amp; CO. ANNOUNCES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THIRD QUARTER 2022 FINANCIAL RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ROLLING MEADOWS, IL, October&nbsp;27, 2022 &#151; Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. (NYSE: AJG) today reported its financial results for the quarter ended
September&nbsp;30, 2022. Management will host a webcast conference call to discuss these results on Thursday, October&nbsp;27, 2022 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to the call, and for printer-friendly formats of this release and the
&#147;CFO Commentary&#148; and &#147;Supplemental Quarterly Data,&#148; which may also be referenced during the call, please visit <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. These documents contain both GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures.
Investors and other users of this information should read carefully the section entitled &#147;Information Regarding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; beginning on page&nbsp;9. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our outstanding performance continued during the third quarter! For our combined brokerage and risk
management segments, total revenues increased 15%, organic revenues increased 8.4%, we completed 6 new mergers, grew net earnings 12%, delivered adjusted EBITDAC margins in excess of 30%, and most importantly, our client-first culture continues to
flourish.&#148; said J. Patrick Gallagher, Jr., Chairman, President and CEO.&nbsp;Through the first nine months of the year, revenues have increased 22%, organic growth is 9.8%, net earnings have grown 25% and adjusted EPS is up 20%. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our third quarter renewal premium data shows global premium increases approximate 10.5%, a bit higher than the renewal premium change in the first half
of the year.&nbsp;Price increases are mostly consistent with recent quarters across nearly all lines of business.&nbsp;Client exposures, including favorable policy endorsements, continue to increase, and new arising claim counts moved higher year
over year; these metrics are not reflective of an economic slowdown in our clients&#146; businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our talented teams remain focused on what they
do best; delivering superior insurance and risk management advice through data driven insights, our vast resources and our niche capabilities.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Reported third quarter 2022 compensation ratio was 1.6 pts higher than third quarter 2021. This increase
reflects increased integration costs and a seasonally higher compensation ratio related to the reinsurance operations acquired in December 2021, workforce related charges, and other roles to service and acquisition earnout related adjustments, as
well as the resumption of merit wage increases and hiring of producers and other roles to service and support higher organic growth, partially offset by lower incentive compensation and foreign exchange movements. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">**</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjusted third quarter 2022 compensation ratio was 0.7 pts lower than third quarter 2021. This decrease
reflects lower incentive compensation offset in part by a seasonally higher compensation ratio related to the reinsurance operations acquired in December 2021, as well as the resumption of merit wage increases and hiring of producers and other roles
to service and support higher organic growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Reported third quarter 2022 operating expense ratio was 0.9 pts lower than third quarter 2021. This decrease
reflects lower workforce and lease termination related charges, as well as savings from office consolidations and professional fees, partially offset by the return of travel, entertainment and other client-related expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">**</TD>

savings from office consolidations and professional fees partially offset by the return of travel, entertainment and other client-related expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In second and third quarters 2022, Gallagher recognized a net favorable U.K. tax impact related to earnout
liability adjustments. In second quarter 2022, Gallagher recognized a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> U.S. state tax benefit that resulted from legal entity restructuring. In first quarter 2022, Gallagher increased its state
effective income tax rate, which resulted in the overall U.S. effective income tax rate increasing from 25% to 26% and caused Gallagher to have additional income tax benefit during the quarter and recognized a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> benefit related to the revaluation of certain deferred income tax assets. In third quarter 2021, Gallagher incurred additional U.K. income tax expense related to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-deductibility</FONT> of some acquisition related adjustments made in the quarter. In second quarter 2021, the U.K. government enacted tax legislation that increases the corporate income tax rate from 19% to 25%
effective in 2023. Gallagher incurred additional income tax expense in the quarter to adjust certain deferred income tax liabilities to the higher income tax rate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Corporate pretax loss includes a net unrealized foreign exchange remeasurement gain of $16.9&nbsp;million in
third quarter 2022 and a net unrealized foreign exchange remeasurement gain of $3.0&nbsp;million in third quarter 2021. Corporate pretax loss includes a net unrealized foreign exchange remeasurement gain of $33.6&nbsp;million in the nine-month
period ended September&nbsp;30, 2022 and a net unrealized foreign exchange remeasurement loss of $2.2&nbsp;million in the nine-month period ended September&nbsp;30, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Interest and banking costs and</B> <B>debt -</B> At September&nbsp;30, 2022, Gallagher had $1,600.0&nbsp;million of borrowings from public debt,
$4,248.0&nbsp;million of borrowings from private placements and $190.0&nbsp;million of short-term borrowings under its line of credit facility. In addition, Gallagher had $245.4&nbsp;million outstanding under a revolving loan facility that provides
funding for premium finance receivables, which are fully collateralized by the underlying premiums held by insurance carriers, and as such are excluded from our debt covenant computations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Clean energy -</B> Consists of the operating results related to our investments in clean coal production plants and royalty income from clean coal licenses
related to Chem-Mod LLC. The production of IRC Section&nbsp;45 clean energy tax credits ceased in December 2021, which reduced the royalty income received by Chem-Mod LLC and net earnings generated by our investments in clean coal production plants.
Additional information regarding these results is available in the &#147;CFO Commentary&#148; at <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisition costs -</B> Consists
mostly of external professional fees and other due diligence costs related to acquisitions. On occasion, Gallagher enters into forward currency hedges for the purchase price of committed, but not yet funded, acquisitions with funding requirements in
currencies other than the U.S. dollar. The gains or losses, if any, associated with these hedge transactions are also included in acquisition costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate - </B>Consists of overhead allocations mostly related to corporate staff compensation, other corporate level activities, and net unrealized
foreign exchange remeasurement. In addition, it includes the tax expense related to partial taxation of foreign earnings, nondeductible executive compensation and entertainment expenses and the tax benefit from vesting of employee equity awards.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Income Taxes</B> - Gallagher allocates the provision for income taxes to its Brokerage and Risk Management segments using the local country statutory
rates. Gallagher&#146;s consolidated effective tax rate for the quarters ended September&nbsp;30, 2022 and 2021 were 18.6% and (3.1)%, respectively. In first quarter of 2022, Gallagher increased its state effective income tax rate, which resulted in
the overall U.S. effective income tax rate increasing from 25% to 26% and caused Gallagher to incur additional income tax expense during the quarter and recognized a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> benefit related to the revaluation
of certain deferred income tax assets to the higher income tax rate. In addition, the production of IRC Section&nbsp;45 clean energy tax credits ceased in December 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Webcast Conference Call</B> - Gallagher will host a webcast conference call on Thursday, October&nbsp;27, 2022 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to
this call, please go to <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. The call will be available for replay at such website for at least 90 days. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Arthur J.
Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co., a global insurance brokerage, risk management and consulting services firm, is
headquartered in Rolling Meadows, Illinois. Gallagher provides these services in approximately 130 countries around the world through its owned operations and a network of correspondent brokers and consultants. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Acquisition related adjustments, which include change in estimated acquisition earnout payables adjustments and
acquisition related compensation charges. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Amortization of intangible assets reflects the amortization of customer/expiration lists, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-compete</FONT> agreements, trade names and other intangible assets acquired through the company&#146;s merger and acquisition strategy, the impact to amortization expense of acquisition valuation adjustments to these
assets as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The impact of foreign currency translation, as applicable. The amounts excluded with respect to foreign currency
translation are calculated by applying current year foreign exchange rates to the same period in the prior year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Income tax related, which represents the impact of a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> U.S. state
tax benefit that resulted from legal entity restructuring in second quarter 2022 and a net favorable U.K. tax impact related to earnout liability adjustments in second and third quarters of 2022. This represents the impact in first quarter 2022 of a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> income tax benefit related to the revaluation of certain deferred income tax assets as a result of a change in our state effective income tax rate. The 2021 values represent the impact in second
quarter 2021 of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> income tax expense associated with the change in the U.K. effective income tax rate from 19% to 25% that is effective in 2023. It also includes the impact of additional U.K. income tax
expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-deductibility</FONT> of some acquisition related adjustments made in third quarter 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss on extinguishment of debt represents costs incurred on the early redemption of the $650&nbsp;million of 2031
Senior Notes, which included the redemption price premium, the unamortized discount amount on the debt issuance and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">write-off</FONT> of all the debt acquisition costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted ratios</B> - Adjusted compensation expense and adjusted operating expense, respectively, each divided
by adjusted revenues. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Earnings Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>EBITDAC</B> <B>and EBITDAC margin </B>- EBITDAC is net earnings before interest, income taxes, depreciation,
amortization and the change in estimated acquisition earnout payables and EBITDAC margin is EBITDAC divided by total revenues (for the Brokerage segment) and revenues before reimbursements (for the Risk Management segment). These measures for the
Brokerage and Risk Management segments provide a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance for the overall business and provide a meaningful way to measure our financial performance on an ongoing basis.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EBITDAC</B> <B>and Adjusted EBITDAC Margin </B>- Adjusted EBITDAC is EBITDAC adjusted to exclude net
gains (losses) on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related adjustments, transaction related costs, legal and income tax related costs and the period-over-period
impact of foreign currency translation, as applicable and Adjusted EBITDAC margin is Adjusted EBITDAC divided by total adjusted revenues (defined above). These measures for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments provide a meaningful
representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance, and are also presented to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(10 of 15) </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EPS and Adjusted Net Earnings </B>- Adjusted net earnings have been adjusted to exclude the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> impact of net gains (losses) on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, the impact of foreign currency translation, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related
adjustments, transaction related costs, amortization of intangible assets, legal and income tax related costs and effective income tax rate impact, as applicable. Adjusted EPS is Adjusted Net Earnings divided by diluted weighted average shares
outstanding. This measure provides a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance (and as such should not be used as a measure of Gallagher&#146;s liquidity), and for the overall business is also presented to improve the
comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. This is the third quarter that we have excluded amortization of intangible assets from adjusted EPS, and as such, we have
provided the same adjustment for the prior period for comparability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organic Revenues (a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure)</B> - For the Brokerage segment, organic change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues exclude the first twelve months of such revenues generated
from acquisitions and such revenues related to divested operations in each year presented.&nbsp;These revenues are excluded from organic revenues in order to help interested persons analyze the revenue growth associated with the operations that were
a part of Gallagher in both the current and prior period.&nbsp;In addition, organic change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues excludes the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation to
improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. For the Risk Management segment, organic change in fee revenues excludes the first twelve months of fee revenues
generated from acquisitions in each year presented. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, change in organic growth excludes the period-over-period impact of foreign currency
translation to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These revenue items are excluded from organic revenues in order to determine a comparable, but <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT> measurement
of revenue growth that is associated with the revenue sources that are expected to continue in the current year and beyond.&nbsp;Gallagher has historically viewed organic revenue growth as an important indicator when assessing and evaluating the
performance of its Brokerage and Risk Management segments.&nbsp;Gallagher also believes that using this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure allows readers of our financial statements to measure, analyze and compare the growth
from our Brokerage and Risk Management segments in a meaningful and consistent manner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Information Presented to GAAP Measures</B> - This press release includes tabular reconciliations to the most comparable GAAP measures, as follows: for EBITDAC (on pages&nbsp;12 and 13), for adjusted
revenues, adjusted EBITDAC and adjusted diluted net earnings per share (on pages&nbsp;1 and 2), for organic revenue measures (on pages&nbsp;3 and 5, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments), for adjusted compensation and
operating expenses and adjusted EBITDAC margin (on pages&nbsp;4, 5 and 6, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(11 of 15) </P>
